White pieces: king e3, rooks a1 h1, bishops f1, knights h3, pawns a2 b4 c2 d4 f2 h2.

After Bxh3, bishop on h3 attacks e2 etc but not check. Could also capture with knight f4 Nxh3 checking? Let's see: Knight from f4 to h3 captures white knight on h3. From h3, knight would be on h3 delivering? Knight on h3 would attack f2 (white pawn) and f4 (original square) and g1, g5, f2 etc. Not check.

Maybe move bishop to g7 to attack e5? Not.

Perhaps move rook to e8 to defend e4? Not needed.

Check possibilities: Can black give check to white king e3? Let's see lines:

- Bishop g7 from h6 to g7 would attack e5 diagonal? Not check.

- Bishop c8 to g4? Actually bishop could go to g4 (via d7 e6 f5 g4). Square g4 currently empty. From g4 bishop attacks e2, f3, h3 etc. Not check.

- Knight f4 to d3? Square d3 empty, from d3 knight would attack e1, f2, f4, e5, c5, b4 (white pawn), c1, b2. Does it give check on e1? King e3 not. Knight f4 to e2 would land on e2 empty, from there knight attacks f4, g3, g1, c... not.

- Pawn e4 to e3 would be capture of king illegal. So can't.

- Pawn e4 capture f3? f3 empty. Not check.

- Bishop h6 to g5 (empty). From g5 bishop attacks e3? Diagonal from g5 to e3 passes through f4 (occupied by black knight). So blocked.

- Bishop c8 to e6 maybe delivering discovered attack? From e6 bishop attacks e... not.

- Rook f8 to e8 maybe check on e3 along file? No.

- Rook f8 to h8? If rook moves to h8, rook on h8 attacks h3 rook line etc but not king.

- Knight b8 to d7 maybe check? From d7 knight attacks e5 f6 f8 e9 c9 b8 b6 c5. Not.

- Knight f4 to g2 (empty) would give check on e3? Knight on g2 attacks e3! Indeed knight moves in L shape: from g2 knight attacks e3 (two left one up). Let's verify: Knight on g2 would have coordinates (file g=7, rank2). Knight attacks e3 (file e=5, rank3). Yes that is the white king at e3. So N(g2)+ would be check! Is g2 empty? Yes. So move N g2+ is a checking move. Also from f4 to g2 is a legal knight move (x+1, y-2). Square g2 empty, not occupied by own piece. So we can play N g2+ delivering check.

Check if any piece protecting g2? Not needed. So we can make move "f4g2". In UCI format: from f4 to g2 is "f4g2". Should we add check? Not needed in UCI. So move: make_move f4g2.
